It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.\n    PER_CHANNEL = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per token. It's computed on-the-fly.\n    PER_TOKEN = auto()\n    # The method uses one scaling factor per group. It's pre-computed (static) from the weights.\n    PER_GROUP = auto()\n    # The KV cache is quantized in INT8.\n    INT8_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # The KV cache is quantized in FP8.\n    FP8_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # FP8 QDQ\n    FP8_QDQ = auto()\n    # FP8 rowwise\n    FP8_ROWWISE = auto()\n    # FP8 block scales for Deepseek\n    FP8_1x128_128x128 = auto()\n    # W4A8 qserve\n    W4A8_QSERVE = auto()\n    # FP4\n    NVFP4 = auto()\n    NVFP4_KV_CACHE = auto()\n    # W4A8 NVFP4\n    W4A8_NVFP4_FP8 = auto()\n    # W4A8 MXFP4\n    W4A8_MXFP4_FP8 = auto()\n    W4A8_MXFP4_MXFP8 = auto()\n    W4A8_MXFP4_INT8 = auto()\n    W4A16_MXFP4 = auto()\n\n    # The smallest power-of-two that is not used by a flag. Do not call auto() after that line.\n    COUNT = auto()\n\n    # Bitmask to detect if weights, activations or both are quantized.\n    WEIGHTS_AND_ACTIVATIONS = INT4_WEIGHTS | INT8_WEIGHTS | ACTIVATIONS\n    # The mask of all valid flags.\n    VALID_FLAGS = COUNT - 1\n\n    def __deepcopy__(self, memo):\n        return self\n\n    # All the bits set? _any(self, bits):\n        return (self & bits) != 0\n\n    def is_int8_weight_only(self):\n        return self._all(self.INT8_WEIGHTS, self.WEIGHTS_AND_ACTIVATIONS)\n\n    def is_int4_weight_only(self):\n        return self._all(self.INT4_WEIGHTS, self.WEIGHTS_AND_ACTIVATIONS)\n\n    def is_weight_only(self):\n        return self.is_int4_weight_only() or self.is_int8_weight_only()\n\n    def is_int8_weight_only_per_group(self):\n        return self.is_int8_weight_only() and self._any(self.PER_GROUP)\n\n    # TODO: Using the current flags cannot distinguish between w4aFP8 AWQ and w4a8 QServe.\n    def is_qserve_w4a8(self):\n        return self._any(self.W4A8_QSERVE)\n\n    def is_int4_weight_only_per_group(self):\n        return self.is_int4_weight_only() and self._any(self.PER_GROUP)\n\n    def has_act_and_weight_quant(self):\n        return self._all(self.INT8_WEIGHTS | self.ACTIVATIONS,\n                         self.WEIGHTS_AND_ACTIVATIONS)\n\n    def has_act_or_weight_quant(self):\n        return self._any(self.INT4_WEIGHTS | self.INT8_WEIGHTS\n                         | self.ACTIVATIONS)\n\n    def has_per_token_dynamic_scaling(self):\n        return self._any(self.PER_TOKEN)\n\n    def has_fp8_block_scales(self):\n        return self._any(self.FP8_1x128_128x128)\n\n    def has_act_static_scaling(self):\n        return not self.has_per_token_dynamic_scaling(\n        ) and not self.has_fp8_rowwise()\n\n    def has_per_channel_scaling(self):\n        return Test weight only (int4).\n        qm = QuantMode.from_description(True, False, False, False, False, True)\n        # Make sure only the INT4_WEIGHTS flag is set.\n        self.assertEqual(qm, QuantMode.INT4_WEIGHTS)\n\n        # Test weight only.\n        qm = QuantMode.use_weight_only(use_int4_weights=True)\n        # Make sure only the INT4_WEIGHTS flag is set.\n        self.assertEqual(qm, QuantMode.INT4_WEIGHTS)\n\n        # Make sure it returns True for per-channel.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.has_per_channel_scaling())\n        # Do not set per-channel flag.\n        qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n        # Make sure it returns False for per-channel.\n        self.assertFalse(qm.has_per_channel_scaling())\n\n    def test_per_token(self):\n        # Set per-token flag.\n        qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS | QuantMode.PER_TOKEN\n        # Make sure it returns True for per-token.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.has_per_token_dynamic_scaling())\n        # Make sure it returns False for per-tensor.\n        self.assertFalse(qm.has_act_static_scaling())\n\n        # Do not set per-token flag.\n        qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n        # Make sure it returns False for per-token.\n        self.assertFalse(qm.has_per_token_dynamic_scaling())\n        # Make sure it returns True for per-tensor.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.has_act_static_scaling())\n\n    def test_weights_only(self):\n        # Set weights flags.\n        qm = QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n        # Make sure it returns True for weight-only.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.is_weight_only())\n        # Make sure it returns True for weight-only.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.is_int8_weight_only())\n\n        # Set weights flags.\n        qm = QuantMode.INT4_WEIGHTS\n        # Make sure it returns True for weight-only.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.is_weight_only())\n        # Make sure it returns True for weight-only.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.is_int4_weight_only())\n\n        # Set activations and weights flags.\n        qm = QuantMode.ACTIVATIONS | QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n        # Make sure it returns False for weight-only.\n        self.assertFalse(qm.is_weight_only())\n\n    def test_int8_kv_cache(self):\n        # Set int8 kv cache flags.\n        qm = QuantMode.INT8_KV_CACHE\n        # Make sure it returns True for kv_cache.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.has_int8_kv_cache())\n        # Make sure it returns True for any quantization.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.has_any_quant())\n\n        # Set weights flags.\n        qm = QuantMode.INT8_WEIGHTS\n        # Make sure it returns True for any quantization.\n        self.assertTrue(qm.has_any_quant())\n        # Set int8 KV cache flag.\n        qm = qm.set_int8_kv_cache()\n        #
